    <script type='text/javascript'>
    var googletag = googletag || {};
    googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
    (function() {
    var gads = document.createElement('script');
    gads.async = true;
    gads.type = 'text/javascript';
    var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;
    gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') +
    '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
    var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
    node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);
    })();
    function adslots() {
      var retailSlots = $("body").find(".adslot").filter(":visible"), i = 0, slotR = new Array();
      var houseSlots = $("body").find(".adslot").filter(":hidden"), j = 0, slotH = new Array();
      if (retailSlots.length || houseSlots.length) {
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
          $(retailSlots).each(function(){
            var adUnit = $(this).attr('data-section') + $(this).attr('data-ad-unit');
            var pageID = $(this).attr('data-pageid');
            
            if (pageID) {
              slotR[i] = googletag.defineSlot('/1017433/'+adUnit, [$(this).width(), $(this).height()], $(this).attr('id')).addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('pageid', [pageID]);
            } else {
              slotR[i] = googletag.defineSlot('/1017433/'+adUnit, [$(this).width(), $(this).height()], $(this).attr('id')).addService(googletag.pubads());
            }
            i++
          });
          $(houseSlots).each(function(){
            var adUnit = 'House' + $(this).attr('data-ad-unit');
            
            slotH[j] = googletag.defineSlot('/1017433/'+adUnit, [$(this).width(), $(this).height()], $(this).attr('id')).addService(googletag.pubads());
            j++
          });
//        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);

          googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

          
          googletag.enableServices();
          $(retailSlots).each(function(){
            googletag.display($(this).attr('id'));
          });
          $(houseSlots).each(function(){
            googletag.display($(this).attr('id'));
          });
          
        });
      } else {
//        console.log('huh, both empty');
      }
    }
    $(document).ready(function(){
      setTimeout(adslots, 200)
    });
    </script>

        <h1 class="festHead">Unofficial Parties &amp; Free Shows</h1>
  <img class="righto" src="/Images/SXSW/sxsw-2019-music.jpg">
  <div style="font-size:14px;line-height:21px;margin-top:6px;">For the badgeless and money-strapped, it's our annual exhaustive (and exhausting) list of unofficial shows. From major venues to your neighbor's backyard, there will be bands playing anywhere and everywhere from the start of SXSW until all the out-of-towners fly back home. We're doing our best to keep this list up-to-date, but, let's face it, artists can be flaky and these shows can be <i>very</i> unofficial, so expect set times and lineups to change at the last minute. Who knows, maybe that random band you see will be your next obsession.</div>
  <div style="font-size:14px;line-height:21px;margin-top:6px;">Got an unofficial show we should know about? Email the details â date, time, location, and band name â to <b>clubs@austinchronicle.com</b>. Please include "SXSW party" in the subject.</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
  var d = new Date();
  d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
  var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
  document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
}
function getCookie(cname) {
  var name = cname + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return "";
}
$(document).ready(function() {
  var hideSupport = getCookie('hideSupport');
  if (hideSupport != "") {
    $('#support-inner').addClass('hide-support-bar');
    $('#final-footer').addClass('hide-support-bar');
  }
  $(window).scroll(function () { 
    if ($(window).scrollTop() > $('body').height() / 4) {
      $('#support-bar').slideDown(500);
    } else {
      $('#support-bar').slideUp(500);
    } 
  });
  $('#close-support-link').click(function(e) {
    $('#support-inner').addClass('hide-support-bar');
    $('#final-footer').addClass('hide-support-bar');
    setCookie("hideSupport", "yes", 2);
    e.preventDefault();
  });
});
</script>

  
<!-- Adblock Detection -->
<script>
var test = document.createElement('div');
test.innerHTML = '&nbsp;';
test.className = 'adsbox';
document.body.appendChild(test);
window.setTimeout(function() {
  if (test.offsetHeight === 0) {

    document.body.classList.add('adblock');
    ga('send', 'event', 'Ad Setting', 'Adblock', 'Enabled');
  }
  test.remove();
}, 400);
</script>
<!--end Adblock Detection -->

<script>
function dotDot() {
  $('.dotdotdot').ellipsis('a', { live: false });

  $('.half-headline-section.dotdotdot').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.half-subhead-section.dotdotdot').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.article-description.dotdotdot').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.archive-description.dotdotdot').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.joint-description').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.module .dsq-widget-thread').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.intro-blog.contest').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.intro-blog.event').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.fifth-item-text.dotdotdot').ellipsis('', { live: false });
  $('.dotdotdot a, a.archive-link').each(function() {
    var titleText = $(this).attr('title');
    if (/<\/i> /.test(titleText)) {
      console.log('got one: '+titleText);
      var htmlString = $(this).html();
      var newString = htmlString.replace(/<\/i>/g,'</i> ');
      $(this).html(newString);
    }
  });
  $('.fifth-item-text.dotdotdot').each(function() {
    var htmlString = $(this).html();
    var newString = htmlString.replace(/<\/span>/g,'</span> ');
    $(this).html(newString);
  });
}
$(document).ready(function() {
  dotDot();
});
$(window).resize(function() {
  setTimeout(dotDot, 200)
});
